│ SOLUTION: The workflow instructions should tell Claude to:
1. Read the base subagent file (e.g., ~/.claude/agents/workflows/code-researcher.md)
2. Execute it AS IF it's a specialized expert with the rendered template providing:
   - Current workflow context
   - Input file locations from previous phases
   - Output deliverable locations
   - Specific task within this workflow phase

This is a "prompt injection" pattern: base expertise + workflow-specific context = customized execution. No Task tool needed - Claude directly embodies the agent with the workflow context.   │
